Here's everything we know about the app's future in the US — and everything we don't.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-everything-we-know-about-video-app-future-in-us-2020-8?utm_source=feedburner&amp;utm_medium=referral","description":"<p><iframe allowfullscreen width=\"1333\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/image/5f32b4b15af6cc2b7c6406d5\" frameborder=\"0\"></iframe></p>\n<p></p><p><img src=\"https://static3.businessinsider.com/image/5f32fcd1988ee36735399d04-2400/trump-tiktok-us-china-trade-war-4x3.png\" border=\"0\" alt=\"trump tiktok us china trade war 4x3\" /><span class=\"source\">Samantha Lee/Business Insider</span></p><p></p>\n<ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>President Donald Trump is threatening to ban popular viral-video app TikTok in the US over claims that it poses a national-security risk through its Chinese parent company ByteDance.</li>\n<li>ByteDance is entertaining TikTok acquisition talks with US tech companies to assuage concerns from the president. Microsoft is the favorite, and a potential deal is valued between $10 billion and $30 billion.</li>\n<li>Trump has issued two executive orders aimed at banning TikTok is recent weeks. Questions remain of the legality of Trump's orders, or whether they're enforceable at all.</li>\n<li>TikTok <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-lawsuit-us-government-trump-ban-due-process-national-security-2020-8?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\">filed suit against the Trump administration Monday</a> over the August 6 executive order that bans \"any transactions\" between Americans and ByteDance beginning in September.</li>\n<li>TikTok alleges the US government failed to afford \"due process\" and has no evidence to back up its national-security claims.</li>\n<li>Here's everything that's happened to threaten TikTok's future in the US, and what we know about what's to come.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\">Visit Business Insider's homepage for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><h3>Lawmakers' concerns about TikTok trace back to when the app first landed in the US in November 2017, when TikTok's parent company ByteDance bought a US-based app called Musical.ly. Musical.ly was shut down in the US a year later, and was merged with TikTok.</h3>\n<img src=\"https://static4.businessinsider.com/image/5f32b4b15af6cc2b7c6406d5/lawmakers-concerns-about-tiktok-trace-back-to-when-the-app-first-landed-in-the-us-in-november-2017-when-tiktoks-parent-company-bytedance-bought-a-us-based-app-called-musically-musically-was-shut-down-in-the-us-a-year-later-and-was-merged-with-tiktok.jpg\" alt=\"\"/><span class=\"source\">Musically</span>\n<p><p>Musical.ly was a watered-down version of TikTok: Its capabilities were limited to creating and sharing 15-second lip sync music videos. ByteDance's acquisition of Musical.ly was valued at $1 billion.</p>\n<p><em>Source: <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-app-online-website-video-sharing-2019-7?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\">Business Insider</a></em></p></p>\n<br/><br/><h3>China has been a target of the US government since Donald Trump took office in 2016. He's blamed China for the spread of the coronavirus pandemic, and accused Chinese companies of using their products to spy on US citizens for the state government.</h3>\n<img src=\"https://static2.businessinsider.com/image/5f32b5760ef1882c79694822/china-has-been-a-target-of-the-us-government-since-donald-trump-took-office-in-2016-hes-blamed-china-for-the-spread-of-the-coronavirus-pandemic-and-accused-chinese-companies-of-using-their-products-to-spy-on-us-citizens-for-the-state-government.jpg\" alt=\"\"/><span class=\"source\">Artyom Ivanov\\TASS via Getty Images</span>\n<br/><br/><h3>As TikTok's popularity soared in 2019, lawmakers took a closer look at the app's ties to China. They've raised concerns of potential risks to US national security, the privacy of young users, and content moderation.</h3>\n<img src=\"https://static4.businessinsider.com/image/5f32b79f505f5364972e8e25/as-tiktoks-popularity-soared-in-2019-lawmakers-took-a-closer-look-at-the-apps-ties-to-china-theyve-raised-concerns-of-potential-risks-to-us-national-security-the-privacy-of-young-users-and-content-moderation.jpg\" alt=\"\"/><span class=\"source\">Joshua Roberts/Reuters</span>\n<p><p>In 2019, TikTok paid out a $5.7 million fine to the Federal Trade Commission to settle allegations it illegally collected personal information from children under age 13 without parental consent.</p>\n<p>Children's privacy advocates have since <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-ftc-complaint-violating-childrens-privacy-2020-5?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"60\">accused TikTok of breaking the terms</a> of the FTC settlement by failing to alter policies, and refusing to delete videos and other content obtained illegally. As a result, the FTC and US Justice Department are now looking into allegations it failed to live up to its 2019 agreement.</p>\n<p>Beyond national security, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tiktok-censorship-users-deemed-ugly-overweight-or-disabled-2020-3?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\">TikTok has faced allegations it censors certain types videos</a>, including content categorized as political, \"culturally problematic,\" and coming from creators the company says are more prone to bullying.</p>\n<p><em>Source: <a class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><a href=\"http://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&amp;u=1088116&amp;m=87714&amp;urllink=yardbird.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored\">Yardbird</a> is an outdoor furniture startup with an environmental conscience, making stylish and affordably priced pieces from intercepted ocean plastic.&nbsp;</li>\n<li>The hand-woven wicker used in Yardbird furniture incorporates plastic collected from beaches in the Philippines.</li>\n<li>It's the company's way of helping you enjoy the outdoors with a material that would otherwise hurt the earth and take away from that enjoyment.&nbsp;</li>\n<li>While comparable sectional sets can cost around $5,000, Yardbird's costs less than $2,500.</li>\n<li>They look just as good and are durable and weather-resistant.&nbsp;</li>\n<li>See more: <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-patio-furniture?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">The best patio furniture</a></li>\n</ul>\n<p>As the weather warms up again, it just doesn't feel right to spend all night after work or all weekend staying cooped up inside.</p>\n<p>We're not saying you need to go far in order to enjoy the warm sun and refreshing breeze. If you have a backyard, you can have a wonderful and relaxing time right outside your home, with a drink and book in hand, or friends and neighbors on speed dial.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Until recently, the new companies entering the direct-to-consumer space focused on all the things that go <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/home-kitchen-bedding-startups-2018-10?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">inside your home</a> &mdash; <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-mattress?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">mattresses</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-sheets?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">sheets</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/brooklinen-bath-collection-towels-review-2018-5?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">towels</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/direct-to-consumer-kitchen-knife-cookware-startups-2018-4?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">cookware</a>, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/campaign-sofa-vs-burrow-couch-which-is-better-2018-10?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">furniture</a>, and the like. Considering we spend the majority of our time indoors, whether we're cooking, sleeping, or relaxing, this makes sense, but if you wanted a new store to improve your outdoor space, it was difficult to find.&nbsp;</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&amp;u=1088116&amp;m=87714&amp;urllink=yardbird.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow sponsored\">Yardbird</a>, founded in 2017 by a father-son duo, is the direct-to-consumer outdoor furniture company you've been looking for. Evidently, it's what other people have been too because it sold out of $1 million worth of inventory less than a month into its launch. In 2018, it sold out of $4 million of inventory a few months into the year.&nbsp;</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&amp;u=1088116&amp;m=87714&amp;urllink=yardbird.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored\"><img src=\"https://static6.businessinsider.com/image/5c9a4c788629136fe14abdc4-800/yardbird-outdoor-furniture-2.jpg\" border=\"0\" alt=\"yardbird outdoor furniture 2\" /></a></p>\n<h2><a href=\"http://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&amp;u=1088116&amp;m=87714&amp;urllink=yardbird.com%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow nofollow sponsored\">Yardbird</a>'s start and how its furniture is made&nbsp;</h2>\n<p>Fascinated by why high-end furniture companies were charging at least $5,000 for an outdoor wicker sectional, cofounder Jay Dillon talked to his father (who had experience in the furniture industry) and eventually ended up in factories in Asia, where over 95% of all outdoor furniture is manufactured. There, he was quoted products at one-seventh the retail price, and he knew there was potential for a business.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>What makes Yardbird even more noteworthy isn't only that it sells high-quality and stylish outdoor furniture for less. It's that the pieces are sustainable, made from intercepted ocean plastic.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>As outdoors lovers who wanted to enjoy these outdoors for years to come, the Minnesota-based founders sought to create products that reduced human impact on the planet. Dillon had heard of <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/products-made-from-recycled-plastic-2018-8?utm_source=feedburner&utm_medium=referral\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">large brands incorporating recycled plastics into their products</a>&nbsp;but discovered the process took too many steps and plastic resale prices were too high.</p>\n<p>Instead, he met directly with plastic experts and established relationships with a recycling plant in the Philippines. Together, they spent three years collecting plastic from beaches, waterways, and other susceptible locations in the Philippines. In 2019, the company incorporated 92<strong>,</strong>000 lbs of plastic into its pieces and packaging.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>\n<p>According to Dillon, this is how the plastic goes from floating by the shore to a piece of Yardbird furniture:&nbsp;\"After the recycling plant processes the plastic, we then ship it to our wicker extrusion plant and make all-weather outdoor resin wicker out of the plastic, and then hand weave it onto the frames.\"&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Though it may look like traditional wicker, Yardbird's wicker contains 50% recycled plastic (it went as high as 64% in 2019) and lasts longer. As an eco-friendly company, Yardbird also partners with <a href=\"https://carbonfund.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Carbon Fund</a> to offset 100% of its carbon footprint, and its packaging contains 50% recycled materials.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Outside of the all-weather wicker, the other components of the furniture are also strong, long-lasting, and backed by <a href=\"http://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=999&amp;u=1088116&amp;m=87714&amp;urllink=yardbird.com%2Fpages%2Fyardbird-warranty\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">impressive warranties</a>.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>The commercial-grade aluminum frames (which come with a 10-year warranty) are lightweight and rust-proof. The foam cushions are comfortable and supportive, and they're covered in a high-performance outdoor textile called <a href=\"https://www.sunbrella.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Sunbrella</a> that's water- and sun-resistant.
